Mouse over the 'Media' menu link.
Click the 'Media: thePlatform mpx settings' menu link.
Switch to the active frame titled 'Media: thePlatform mpx settings dialog'.
Check if the 'Connect to MPX' button is present. If not then MPX has not been previously enabled.
Get all the selected import account options and store to a list.
Click the 'Close Overlay X'.

Click the 'Add content type' menu link.
